## Multilens Translation Atlas

### AQM

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[\rho_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \Phi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}}(\rho_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-), \qquad \Phi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}} = \mathsf O_{\texttt{olorol}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{otedolor}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{otoldy}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{qotolol}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{olkory}} \circ \mathsf O_{\texttt{p!!!oldshedy}}\]

  Variable legend: `rho^-` incoming folio line state; `rho^+` outgoing line state; `Phi_line^(AQM)` source operator chain.
  Reading: settle phase / fluid conduit / return gate line.
  Confidence: strong

  Variable legend: `u` is the wave profile; `U_line` is the contraction-compatible update.
  Reading: settle phase / fluid conduit / return gate line.
  Confidence: strong

### Tarot

- `P.1`
  Frame: The Magician
  Movement: Let the fraction settle, then route through the return gate, keeping the line aligned with maintenance protocol sustaining stable circulation over extended time periods.
  Reading: settle phase / fluid conduit / return gate line.

## Direct Operational Meaning

A long-form convergence log: the page encodes "how to keep a living circulation stable over time" — segment the loop, clamp it, and keep returning to the same attractor until the final seal can hold. Process statistics: 91 circulation commands (qo-); 9 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 6 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy).

## Mathematical Extraction

Across the formal lenses, `f79v` behaves as a fixed-point purification page with N_qo=80, N_valve=12, and N_seal=1. The governing update is x_(n+1) = V(C(x_n)); stop when ||x_(n+1)-x_n|| <= eps, then publish y = S(x_*).

## Mythic Extraction

`f79v` is a bathhouse-laboratory chamber: descend through linked pools, purify by circulation, prove stability at the clamps, and only then carry the living fluid onward.

## All-Lens Zero Point

`A long-form convergence log: the page encodes "how to keep a living circulation stable over time" — segment the loop, clamp it, and keep returning to the same attractor until the final seal can hold.`

\[g = \mathrm{Coll}(X), \qquad X = \mathrm{Expand}(g) \oplus r\]

### Typed State Machine

\[
\mathcal R_{f79v} = \{r_{charge}, r_{circulate}, r_{clamp}, r_{commit}, r_{seal}\}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{charge})=r_{circulate}, \qquad
\delta(r_{circulate})=r_{clamp}, \qquad
\delta(r_{clamp})=
\begin{cases}
r_{circulate} & \text{if } \Delta_n > 0 \\
r_{commit} & \text{if } \Delta_n = 0
\end{cases}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{commit})=
\begin{cases}
r_{seal} & \text{if } P_{salt} = 1 \\
r_{circulate} & \text{otherwise}
\end{cases}
\]
